muſt vnderſtande flower herbes thinges reherſed foūd together one time ſeaſon wherefore ſaid licour made one tyme beginnyng firſte ſeconde weeke maie ſhall leaſt ende september october ye make ende therefore muſt gather tyme tyme eche thing ſeaſon maie get put ſome veſſell euery one ſelues thynges thei ought ioyned maner aboue ſaied vſe dreſſe trimme ſaid thynges accordyng tyme maie get yet auncient writer chriſocolla naturall artificiall plini dioſcorides write men vſe phiſicke alſo ſowder gold syluer metalles men vſe yet nowe dayes nature melte reſolue quickely anye ſouderynge vſed worke alſo make bodye ſaye gather together fylynge golde ſiluer thinges wherein man hath neede quicke ſodayne foundinge meltinge moreouer gentlewemen helpe theim ſelues alſo muche make theim fayre maketh ſkinne white fine cleane without daunger poyſon hurtinge teeth fleſhe auncient men olde time grene whereof nowe dayes none founde yet anye man maketh marye haue white alſoo ſomewhat blacke whiche peraduenture man may ſay like theyr grene white little longe piece certayne ſynewes veines longe ſo like vnto roche alome many deceiued deceiue whan man ſetteth ſaied borar vpon fyre boyleth
